### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Arquitetura de Microsserviços

## 1. Documento de Arquitetura (ADR-001)

```markdown
# ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços V11

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead V11 Core

## CONTEXTO:
A versão V11 do DIYAPP precisa evoluir de uma arquitetura monolítica para microsserviços para:
1. Permitir escalabilidade independente de componentes
2. Facilitar deploy contínuo sem downtime
3. Isolar falhas e melhorar resiliência
4. Permitir que diferentes squads trabalhem autonomamente
5. Suportar múltiplas linguagens/frameworks por serviço

**Forças em jogo:**
- Necessidade de 100% uptime em produção
- Equipes distribuídas trabalhando em paralelo
- Complexidade crescente do domínio
- Requisitos de performance variados por funcionalidade

## DECISÃO:
Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços com os seguintes princípios:
1. **Serviços por Domínio:** Cada microsserviço encapsula um domínio de negócio completo
2. **Comunicação:** gRPC para comunicação síncrona entre serviços, Eventos (Kafka) para comunicação assíncrona
3. **API Gateway:** Único ponto de entrada para clientes externos
4. **Service Mesh:** Istio para gerenciamento de tráfego, observabilidade e segurança
5. **Banco de Dados:** Database-per-service pattern com eventual consistency via eventos
6. **Observabilidade:** Centralizada com OpenTelemetry, Prometheus e Grafana

## OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:

### Opção A: Monólito Modularizado
- **Prós:** Simplicidade inicial, transações ACID fáceis, deploy único
- **Contras:** Escalabilidade limitada, acoplamento alto, deploy de risco
- **Rejeitada:** Não atende requisitos de escalabilidade e autonomia das squads

### Opção B: Microsserviços Leves (REST + RabbitMQ)
- **Prós:** Mais simples que gRPC, ampla adoção, ferramentas maduras
- **Contras:** Overhead de HTTP/JSON, sem streaming nativo, contratos frágeis
- **Rejeitada:** Performance inferior para comunicação interna

### Opção C: Microsserviços V11 (gRPC + Kafka + Istio) - ESCOLHIDA
- **Prós:** 
  - gRPC: Performance 7-10x melhor que REST, streaming bidirecional, contratos fortes com Protobuf
  - Kafka: Alta throughput, retenção de eventos, reprocessamento
  - Istio: Observabilidade nativa, circuit breaking, mTLS automático
- **Contras:** 
  - Curva de aprendizado mais íngreme
  - Complexidade operacional aumentada
  - Necessidade de infraestrutura mais robusta

## CONSEQUÊNCIAS:

### Positivas:
1. Escalabilidade horizontal independente por serviço
2. Deploys independentes e frequentes
3. Isolamento de falhas - problema em um serviço não derruba o sistema
4. Poliglotismo - cada squad escolhe a melhor stack para seu domínio
5. Observabilidade granular por serviço

### Negativas (trade-offs aceitos):
1. Complexidade distribuída (transações distribuídas, eventual consistency)
2. Overhead de rede e serialização
3. Necessidade de infraestrutura mais complexa (Service Mesh, Message Broker)
4. Debug mais difícil (necessidade de tracing distribuído)

### Riscos e Mitigações:
1. **Latência de rede:** Implementar caching estratégico e circuit breakers
2. **Consistência eventual:** Usar padrões SAGA e compensação
3. **Gestão de configuração:** HashiCorp Vault para secrets, ConfigMaps para configurações
4. **Monitoramento:** Implementar health checks, métricas e alertas por serviço

## REVISÃO:
Reavaliar em 6 meses (2024-07-15) ou após 1M de usuários ativos
```

## 3. Arquivos Principais do Template

### 3.1 `.github/workflows/ci.yml`
```yaml
name: CI Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main, develop ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]

jobs:
  test:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    services:
      postgres:
        image: postgres:14
        env:
          POSTGRES_PASSWORD: postgres
        options: >-
          --health-cmd pg_isready
          --health-interval 10s
          --health-timeout 5s
          --health-retries 5
        ports:
          - 5432:5432
      kafka:
        image: confluentinc/cp-kafka:latest
        env:
          KAFKA_ZOOKEEPER_CONNECT: localhost:2181
          KAFKA_ADVERTISED_LISTENERS: PLAINTEXT://localhost:9092
        ports:
          - 9092:9092

    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Set up Go
      uses: actions/setup-go@v4
      with:
        go-version: '1.21'
    
    - name: Install dependencies
      run: go mod download
    
    - name: Run linter
      run: |
        go install github.com/golangci/golangci-lint/cmd/golangci-lint@latest
        golangci-lint run --timeout 5m
    
    - name: Run unit tests
      run: go test ./... -v -coverprofile=coverage.out
    
    - name: Run integration tests
      run: |
        go test ./tests/integration -v -tags=integration
        timeout: 10m
    
    - name: Upload coverage to Codecov
      uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
      with:
        file: ./coverage.out

  build:
    needs: test
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Set up Docker Buildx
      uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v2
    
    - name: Build and push
      uses: docker/build-push-action@v4
      with:
        context: .
        push: false
        tags: diyapp/${{ github.event.repository.name }}:latest
        cache-from: type=gha
        cache-to: type=gha,mode=max
```

### 3.2 `.github/workflows/cd.yml`
```yaml
name: CD Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches:
      - main
      - release/*

jobs:
  deploy-staging:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment: staging
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/main'
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Configure AWS credentials
      uses: aws-actions/configure-aws-credentials@v2
      with:
        aws-access-key-id: ${{ secrets.AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID }}
        aws-secret-access-key: ${{ secrets.AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY }}
        aws-region: us-east-1
    
    - name: Login to ECR
      id: login-ecr
      uses: aws-actions/amazon-ecr-login@v1
    
    - name: Build, tag, and push image
      env:
        ECR_REGISTRY: ${{ steps.login-ecr.outputs.registry }}
        ECR_REPOSITORY: ${{ github.event.repository.name }}
        IMAGE_TAG: ${{ github.sha }}
      run: |
        docker build -t $ECR_REGISTRY/$ECR_REPOSITORY:$IMAGE_TAG .
        docker push $ECR_REGISTRY/$ECR_REPOSITORY:$IMAGE_TAG
    
    - name: Deploy to EKS
      run: |
        aws eks update-kubeconfig --name diyapp-staging
        kubectl set image deployment/${{ github.event.repository.name }} \
          ${{ github.event.repository.name }}=$ECR_REGISTRY/$ECR_REPOSITORY:$IMAGE_TAG \
          -n diyapp-staging

  deploy-production:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    environment: production
    needs: deploy-staging
    if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/heads/release/')
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Deploy to production
      run: |
        # Implementar blue-green deployment com Istio
        ./scripts/deploy-production.sh ${{ github.sha }}
```

### 3.3 `src/proto/service.proto`
```protobuf
syntax = "proto3";

package diyapp.v11;

option go_package = "github.com/diyapp/v11/proto";

import "google/protobuf/timestamp.proto";
import "google/api/annotations.proto";

service UserService {
  rpc GetUser(GetUserRequest) returns (UserResponse) {
    option (google.api.http) = {
      get: "/v1/users/{user_id}"
    };
  }
  
  rpc CreateUser(CreateUserRequest) returns (UserResponse) {
    option (google.api.http) = {
      post: "/v1/users"
      body: "*"
    };
  }
  
  rpc StreamUsers(StreamUsersRequest) returns (stream UserResponse);
}

message GetUserRequest {
  string user_id = 1;
}

message CreateUserRequest {
  string email = 1;
  string name = 2;
  map<string, string> metadata = 3;
}

message UserResponse {
  string id = 1;
  string email = 2;
  string name = 3;
  google.protobuf.Timestamp created_at = 4;
  google.protobuf.Timestamp updated_at = 5;
  Status status = 6;
  
  enum Status {
    ACTIVE = 0;
    INACTIVE = 1;
    SUSPENDED = 2;
  }
}

message StreamUsersRequest {
  int32 batch_size = 1;
  string filter = 2;
}
```

### 3.4 `src/server/server.go`
```go
package main

import (
	"context"
	"log"
	"net"
	"os"
	"os/signal"
	"syscall"
	"time"

	"google.golang.org/grpc"
	"google.golang.org/grpc/health"
	"google.golang.org/grpc/health/grpc_health_v1"
	"google.golang.org/grpc/reflection"

	"github.com/diyapp/v11/proto"
	"github.com/diyapp/v11/src/domain/services"
	"github.com/diyapp/v11/src/infrastructure/database"
	"github.com/diyapp/v11/src/infrastructure/messaging"
	"go.opentelemetry.io/contrib/instrumentation/google.golang.org/grpc/otelgrpc"
)

type server struct {
	proto.UnimplementedUserServiceServer
	userService services.UserService
	kafkaProducer *messaging.KafkaProducer
}

func (s *server) GetUser(ctx context.Context, req *proto.GetUserRequest) (*proto.UserResponse, error) {
	// Implementação
	return &proto.UserResponse{}, nil
}

func main() {
	// Configuração
	port := os.Getenv("PORT")
	if port == "" {
		port = "50051"
	}

	// Conexão com banco de dados
	db, err := database.NewPostgresConnection()
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to connect to database: %v", err)
	}
	defer db.Close()

	// Kafka Producer
	producer, err := messaging.NewKafkaProducer()
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to create Kafka producer: %v", err)
	}
	defer producer.Close()

	// Serviços
	userRepo := database.NewUserRepository(db)
	userService := services.NewUserService(userRepo)

	// Servidor gRPC com OpenTelemetry
	srv := grpc.NewServer(
		grpc.UnaryInterceptor(otelgrpc.UnaryServerInterceptor()),
		grpc.StreamInterceptor(otelgrpc.StreamServerInterceptor()),
	)

	// Registrar serviços
	proto.RegisterUserServiceServer(srv, &server{
		userService:   userService,
		kafkaProducer: producer,
	})

	// Health checks
	healthServer := health.NewServer()
	grpc_health_v1.RegisterHealthServer(srv, healthServer)
	healthServer.SetServingStatus("", grpc_health_v1.HealthCheckResponse_SERVING)

	// Reflection para debugging
	reflection.Register(srv)

	// Iniciar servidor
	lis, err := net.Listen("tcp", ":"+port)
	if err != nil {
		log.Fatalf("Failed to listen: %v", err)
	}

	go func() {
		log.Printf("Server starting on port %s", port)
		if err := srv.Serve(lis); err != nil {
			log.Fatalf("Failed to serve: %v", err)
		}
	}()

	// Graceful shutdown
	stop := make(chan os.Signal, 1)
	signal.Notify(stop, syscall.SIGINT, syscall.SIGTERM)
	<-stop

	log.Println("Shutting down server...")
	
	// Dar tempo para conexões terminarem
	ctx, cancel := context.WithTimeout(context.Background(), 30*time.Second)
	defer cancel()
	
	srv.GracefulStop()
	healthServer.Shutdown()
	
	log.Println("Server stopped gracefully")
}
```

### 3.5 `deployments/k8s/deployment.yaml`
```yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: user-service
  namespace: diyapp-production
  labels:
    app: user-service
    version: v1
    part-of: diyapp-v11
spec:
  replicas: 3
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: user-service
  strategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
    rollingUpdate:
      maxSurge: 1
      maxUnavailable: 0
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: user-service
        version: v1
      annotations:
        sidecar.istio.io/inject: "true"
        prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
        prometheus.io/port: "9090"
    spec:
      serviceAccountName: user-service-sa
      containers:
      - name: user-service
        image: ecr.amazonaws.com/diyapp/user-service:latest
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        ports:
        - containerPort: 50051
          name: grpc
        - containerPort: 9090
          name: metrics
        - containerPort: 8080
          name: http
        env:
        - name: ENVIRONMENT
          value: "production"
        - name: DATABASE_URL
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: database-secrets
              key: url
        - name: KAFKA_BROKERS
          value: "kafka-cluster:9092"
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "256Mi"
            cpu: "250m"
          limits:
            memory: "512Mi"
            cpu: "500m"
        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health
            port: 8080
          initialDelaySeconds: 30
          periodSeconds: 10
        readinessProbe:
          exec:
            command:
            - /bin/grpc_health_probe
            - -addr=:50051
          initialDelaySeconds: 5
          periodSeconds: 5
        volume

## 2. .env.example

```env
# Server
NODE_ENV=development
PORT=3000
API_VERSION=v1
API_PREFIX=/api

# Database
DB_HOST=localhost
DB_PORT=5432
DB_NAME=diyapp_v11
DB_USER=diyapp_user
DB_PASSWORD=secure_password_123
DB_POOL_MAX=20
DB_POOL_MIN=5
DB_POOL_IDLE=10000
DB_POOL_ACQUIRE=30000

# Redis
REDIS_HOST=localhost
REDIS_PORT=6379
REDIS_PASSWORD=
REDIS_TTL=3600

# JWT

JWT_EXPIRES_IN=24h

# Rate Limiting

RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS=100

# Bull Queue

QUEUE_REDIS_PORT=6379
QUEUE_CONCURRENCY=5

# Metrics
METRICS_PORT=9090
```

## 3. docker-compose.yml

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-postgres
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp_v11
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp_user
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: secure_password_123
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./src/database/migrations:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp_user"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    container_name: diyapp-redis
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  app:
    build: .
    container_name: diyapp-core
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: production
      DB_HOST: postgres
      REDIS_HOST: redis
      QUEUE_REDIS_HOST: redis
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
      - "9090:9090"
    volumes:
      - ./logs:/app/logs
    restart: unless-stopped

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  redis_data:
```

## 4. Dockerfile

```dockerfile
FROM node:18-alpine

WORKDIR /app

# Install dependencies
COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

# Copy source code
COPY . .

# Create logs directory
RUN mkdir -p /app/logs

# Expose ports
EXPOSE 3000 9090

# Health check
HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \
  CMD node -e "require('http').get('http://localhost:3000/api/v1/health', (r) => {process.exit(r.statusCode === 200 ? 0 : 1)})"

# Start application
CMD ["npm", "start"]
```

## 5. src/index.js

```javascript
const server = require('./server');
const config = require('./config');
const logger = require('./utils/logger');
const database = require('./database');
const cache = require('./cache/redis');
const queue = require('./queue');

async function startServer() {
  try {
    // Initialize database connection
    await database.connect();
    logger.info('Database connected successfully');

    // Initialize Redis cache
    await cache.connect();
    logger.info('Redis cache connected successfully');

    // Initialize Bull queue
    await queue.initialize();
    logger.info('Bull queue initialized successfully');

    // Start server
    const app = server();
    const port = config.port || 3000;

    app.listen(port, () => {
      logger.info(`Server running on port ${port}`);
      logger.info(`API Documentation: http://localhost:${port}/api-docs`);
      logger.info(`Metrics: http://localhost:${port}/metrics`);
    });

    // Graceful shutdown
    const gracefulShutdown = async () => {
      logger.info('Received shutdown signal, closing connections...');
      
      await database.disconnect();
      await cache.disconnect();
      await queue.shutdown();
      
      process.exit(0);
    };

    process.on('SIGTERM', gracefulShutdown);
    process.on('SIGINT', gracefulShutdown);

  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Failed to start server:', error);
    process.exit(1);
  }
}

startServer();
```

## 6. src/server.js

```javascript
const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const compression = require('compression');
const swaggerUi = require('swagger-ui-express');
const swaggerJsdoc = require('swagger-jsdoc');
const promBundle = require('express-prom-bundle');

const config = require('./config');
const apiRoutes = require('./api');
const errorHandler = require('./middleware/errorHandler');
const rateLimiter = require('./middleware/rateLimiter');
const logger = require('./utils/logger');
const metrics = require('./utils/metrics');

// Swagger configuration
const swaggerOptions = {
  definition: {
    openapi: '3.0.0',
    info: {
      title: 'DIYAPP V11 Core API',
      version: '1.0.0',
      description: 'Project Management Service API Documentation',
    },
    servers: [
      {
        url: `http://localhost:${config.port}/api/v1`,
        description: 'Development server',
      },
    ],
    components: {
      securitySchemes: {
        bearerAuth: {
          type: 'http',
          scheme: 'bearer',
          bearerFormat: 'JWT',
        },
      },
      schemas: {
        Project: {
          type: 'object',
          required: ['name', 'description'],
          properties: {
            id: {
              type: 'string',
              format: 'uuid',
              description: 'Project ID',
            },
            name: {
              type: 'string',
              description: 'Project name',
            },
            description: {
              type: 'string',
              description: 'Project description',
            },
            status: {
              type: 'string',
              enum: ['pending', 'active', 'completed', 'archived'],
              default: 'pending',
            },
            metadata: {
              type: 'object',
              description: 'Additional project metadata',
            },
            createdAt: {
              type: 'string',
              format: 'date-time',
            },
            updatedAt: {
              type: 'string',
              format: 'date-time',
            },
          },
        },
        Error: {
          type: 'object',
          properties: {
            error: {
              type: 'string',
              description: 'Error message',
            },
            code: {
              type: 'string',
              description: 'Error code',
            },
            correlationId: {
              type: 'string',
              description: 'Request correlation ID',
            },
          },
        },
      },
    },
  },
  apis: ['./src/api/v1/**/*.js'],
};

const swaggerSpec = swaggerJsdoc(swaggerOptions);

// Prometheus metrics middleware
const metricsMiddleware = promBundle({
  includeMethod: true,
  includePath: true,
  includeStatusCode: true,
  includeUp: true,
  customLabels: { project: 'diyapp-v11-core' },
  promClient: {
    collectDefaultMetrics: {},
  },
});

function createServer() {
  const app = express();

  // Security middleware
  app.use(helmet());
  app.use(cors({
    origin: config.corsOrigin || '*',
    credentials: true,
  }));

  // Compression
  app.use(compression());

  // Body parsing
  app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
  app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true, limit: '10mb' }));

  // Request logging
  app.use((req, res, next) => {
    const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'] || require('crypto').randomUUID();
    req.correlationId = correlationId;
    
    logger.info('Incoming request', {
      correlationId,
      method: req.method,
      url: req.url,
      ip: req.ip,
      userAgent: req.get('User-Agent'),
    });

    res.setHeader('X-Correlation-ID', correlationId);
    next();
  });

  // Metrics
  app.use(metricsMiddleware);
  app.get('/metrics', metrics.metricsHandler);

  // Rate limiting
  app.use('/api/', rateLimiter);

  // API Documentation
  app.use('/api-docs', swaggerUi.serve, swaggerUi.setup(swaggerSpec));

  // Health check endpoint
  app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
    res.status(200).json({
      status: 'healthy',
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      uptime: process.uptime(),
    });
  });

  // API Routes
  app.use('/api', apiRoutes);

  // 404 handler
  app.use((req, res) => {
    res.status(404).json({
      error: 'Not Found',
      message: `Cannot ${req.method} ${req.url}`,
      correlationId: req.correlationId,
    });
  });

  // Error handling
  app.use(errorHandler);

  return app;
}

module.exports = createServer;
```

```javascript
require('dotenv').config();

const config = {
  // Server
  env: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
  port: parseInt(process.env.PORT, 10) || 3000,
  apiVersion: process.env.API_VERSION || 'v1',
  apiPrefix: process.env.API_PREFIX || '/api',
  corsOrigin: process.env.CORS_ORIGIN || '*',

  // Database
  database: {
    host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
    port: parseInt(process.env.DB_PORT, 10) || 5432,
    name: process.env.DB_NAME || 'diyapp_v11',
    user: process.env.DB_USER || 'diyapp_user',
    password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD || 'secure_password_123',
    pool: {
      max: parseInt(process.env.DB_POOL_MAX, 10) || 20,
      min: parseInt(process.env.DB_POOL_MIN, 10) || 5,
      idle: parseInt(process.env.DB_POOL_IDLE, 10) || 10000,
      acquire: parseInt(process.env.DB_POOL_ACQUIRE, 10) || 30000,
    },
  },

  // Redis
  redis: {
    host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
    port: parseInt(process.env.REDIS_PORT, 10) || 6379,
    password: process.env.REDIS_PASSWORD || '',
    ttl: parseInt(process.env.REDIS_TTL, 10) || 3600,
  },

  // JWT
  jwt: {
    secret: process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'your_super_secret_jwt_key_change_in_production',
    expiresIn: process.env.JWT_EXPIRES_IN || '24h',
  },

  // Rate Limiting
  rateLimit: {
    windowMs: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS, 10) || 900000,
    maxRequests: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS, 10) || 100,
  },

  // Bull Queue
  queue: {
    redis: {
      host: process.env.QUEUE_REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
      port: parseInt(process.env.QUEUE_REDIS_PORT, 10) || 6379,
    },
    concurrency: parseInt(process.env.QUEUE_CONCURRENCY, 10) || 5,
  },

  // Metrics
  metrics: {
    port: parseInt(process.env.METRICS_PORT, 10) || 9090,
  },
};

// Validate required configuration
if (!config.database.password || config.database.password === 'secure_password_123') {
  console.warn('WARNING: Using default database password. Change it in production!');
}

if (!config.jwt.secret || config.j

      '@contexts': path.resolve(__dirname, './src/contexts'),
      '@design-system': path.resolve(__dirname, './src/design-system'),

// Design System Tokens - NUNCA valores hardcoded
export const tokens = {
  colors: {
    primary: {
      50: '#eff6ff',
      100: '#dbeafe',
      200: '#bfdbfe',
      300: '#93c5fd',
      400: '#60a5fa',
      500: '#3b82f6',
      600: '#2563eb',
      700: '#1d4ed8',
      800: '#1e40af',
      900: '#1e3a8a',
    },
    neutral: {
      50: '#f8fafc',
      100: '#f1f5f9',
      200: '#e2e8f0',
      300: '#cbd5e1',
      400: '#94a3b8',
      500: '#64748b',
      600: '#475569',
      700: '#334155',
      800: '#1e293b',
      900: '#0f172a',
    },
    success: {
      50: '#f0fdf4',
      500: '#10b981',
      700: '#047857',
    },
    warning: {
      50: '#fffbeb',
      500: '#f59e0b',
      700: '#b45309',
    },
    error: {
      50: '#fef2f2',
      500: '#ef4444',
      700: '#b91c1c',
    },
    background: {
      default: '#f8fafc',
      paper: '#ffffff',
      sidebar: '#1e293b',
    },
  },
  spacing: {
    xs: '0.5rem',    // 8px
    sm: '0.75rem',   // 12px
    md: '1rem',      // 16px
    lg: '1.5rem',    // 24px
    xl: '2rem',      // 32px
    '2xl': '3rem',   // 48px
    '3xl': '4rem',   // 64px
  },
  typography: {
    fontFamily: "'Inter', system-ui, -apple-system, sans-serif",
    fontSize: {
      xs: '0.75rem',    // 12px
      sm: '0.875rem',   // 14px
      base: '1rem',     // 16px
      lg: '1.125rem',   // 18px
      xl: '1.25rem',    // 20px
      '2xl': '1.5rem',  // 24px
      '3xl': '1.875rem', // 30px
      '4xl': '2.25rem',  // 36px
    },
    fontWeight: {
      normal: 400,
      medium: 500,
      semibold: 600,
      bold: 700,
    },
    lineHeight: {
      tight: 1.25,
      normal: 1.5,
      relaxed: 1.75,
    },
  },
  borderRadius: {
    sm: '0.25rem',   // 4px
    md: '0.5rem',    // 8px
    lg: '0.75rem',   // 12px
    xl: '1rem',      // 16px
    full: '9999px',
  },
  shadows: {
    sm: '0 1px 2px 0 rgb(0 0 0 / 0.05)',
    md: '0 4px 6px -1px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
    lg: '0 10px 15px -3px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
    xl: '0 20px 25px -5px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
  },
  zIndex: {
    dropdown: 1000,
    sticky: 1020,
    modal: 1050,
    popover: 1070,
    tooltip: 1080,
  },
} as const

export type ColorToken = keyof typeof tokens.colors
export type SpacingToken = keyof typeof tokens.spacing
export type TypographyToken = keyof typeof tokens.typography

## 14. src/types/index.ts

```typescript
export interface User {
  id: string
  email: string
  name: string
  avatar?: string
  role: 'admin' | 'user' | 'viewer'
  createdAt: Date
}

export interface Project {
  id: string
  name: string
  description: string
  status: 'draft' | 'in_progress' | 'review' | 'completed'
  progress: number
  ownerId: string
  collaborators: string[]
  createdAt: Date
  updatedAt: Date
  dueDate?: Date
}

export interface AuthState {
  user: User | null
  isLoading: boolean
  error: string | null
  isAuthenticated: boolean
}

export interface ProjectsState {
  projects: Project[]
  currentProject: Project | null
  isLoading: boolean
  error: string | null
}

export type ThemeMode = 'light' | 'dark'
export type Language = 'pt' | 'en' | 'es'
```

import { User, AuthState } from '@/types'

interface AuthContextType extends AuthState {
  login: (email: string, password: string) => Promise<void>
  logout: () => Promise<void>
  register: (email: string, password: string, name: string) => Promise<void>

    user: null,
    isLoading: true,
    error: null,
    isAuthenticated: false,

    // Simulate auth check on mount

      if (token) {
        setState({
          user: mockUser,
          isLoading: false,
          error: null,
          isAuthenticated: true,
        })
      } else {
        setState(prev => ({ ...prev, isLoading: false }))
      }
    }, 500)

    return () => clearTimeout(timer)
  }, [])

      // Simulate API call
      await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000))

        localStorage.setItem('diyapp_token', 'mock-jwt-token')

          user: mockUser,

  cluster_endpoint_private_access = true

    "audit",
    "authenticator",
    "controllerManager",
    "scheduler"
  ]

  # Managed Node Groups for critical system components
  eks_managed_node_groups = {
    system = {
      name           = "system"
      instance_types = ["t3.medium"]
      min_size       = 2
      max_size       = 4
      desired_size   = 2

      labels = {
        role = "system"
      }

      taints = {
        dedicated = {
          key    = "role"
          value  = "system"
          effect = "NO_SCHEDULE"
        }
      }

      tags = {
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/enabled"             = "true"
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/diyapp-v11" = "owned"
      }
    }
  }

  # Karpenter for workload nodes (cost optimization)
  enable_karpenter = true

  node_security_group_additional_rules = {
    ingress_self_all = {
      description = "Node to node all ports/protocols"
      protocol    = "-1"
      from_port   = 0
      to_port     = 0
      type        = "ingress"
      self        = true
    }
    egress_all = {
      description      = "Node all egress"
      protocol         = "-1"
      from_port        = 0
      to_port          = 0
      type             = "egress"
      cidr_blocks      = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
      ipv6_cidr_blocks = ["::/0"]
    }
  }

  tags = {
    Environment = var.environment
  }

# Karpenter Provisioner for workload nodes
resource "kubectl_manifest" "karpenter_provisioner" {
  yaml_body = <<-YAML
  apiVersion: karpenter.sh/v1alpha5
  kind: Provisioner
  metadata:
    name: default
  spec:
    requirements:
      - key: "karpenter.sh/capacity-type"
        operator: In
        values: ["spot", "on-demand"]
      - key: "kubernetes.io/arch"
        operator: In
        values: ["amd64", "arm64"]
      - key: "kubernetes.io/os"
        operator: In
        values: ["linux"]
    limits:
      resources:
        cpu: 100
        memory: 100Gi
    providerRef:
      name: default
    ttlSecondsAfterEmpty: 60
    consolidation:
      enabled: true
  YAML

  depends_on = [module.eks]
}

resource "kubectl_manifest" "karpenter_node_template" {
  yaml_body = <<-YAML
  apiVersion: karpenter.k8s.aws/v1alpha1
  kind: AWSNodeTemplate
  metadata:
    name: default
  spec:
    subnetSelector:
      karpenter.sh/discovery: diyapp-v11
    securityGroupSelector:
      karpenter.sh/discovery: diyapp-v11
    tags:
      Project: DIYAPP-V11
      Environment: ${var.environment}
      ManagedBy: Terraform
      KarpenterProvisioned: "true"
    blockDeviceMappings:
      - deviceName: /dev/xvda
        ebs:
          volumeSize: 50Gi
          volumeType: gp3
          encrypted: true
          deleteOnTermination: true
  YAML

  depends_on = [module.eks]
}

# S3 bucket for Prometheus long-term storage
resource "aws_s3_bucket" "prometheus_storage" {
  bucket = "diyapp-prometheus-${var.environment}-${random_id.bucket_suffix.hex}"
  
  tags = {
    Purpose = "Prometheus long-term storage"
  }
}

resource "aws_s3_bucket_versioning" "prometheus_storage" {
  bucket = aws_s3_bucket.prometheus_storage.id
  versioning_configuration {
    status = "Enabled"
  }
}

resource "random_id" "bucket_suffix" {
  byte_length = 8
}

# IAM role for Prometheus to write to S3
resource "aws_iam_role" "prometheus_s3_role" {
  name = "diyapp-prometheus-s3-role"

  assume_role_policy = jsonencode({
    Version = "2012-10-17"
    Statement = [
      {
        Action = "sts:AssumeRoleWithWebIdentity"
        Effect = "Allow"
        Principal = {
          Federated = module.eks.oidc_provider_arn
        }
        Condition = {
          StringEquals = {
            "${module.eks.oidc_provider}:sub" = "system:serviceaccount:monitoring:prometheus-server"
            "${module.eks.oidc_provider}:aud" = "sts.amazonaws.com"
          }
        }
      }
    ]
  })
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy" "prometheus_s3_policy" {
  name = "diyapp-prometheus-s3-policy"
  role = aws_iam_role.prometheus_s3_role.id

  policy = jsonencode({
    Version = "2012-10-17"
    Statement = [
      {
        Action = [
          "s3:ListBucket",
          "s3:PutObject",
          "s3:GetObject",
          "s3:DeleteObject"
        ]
        Effect = "Allow"
        Resource = [
          aws_s3_bucket.prometheus_storage.arn,
          "${aws_s3_bucket.prometheus_storage.arn}/*"
        ]
      }
    ]
  })
}

# Kubernetes provider for monitoring stack

  host                   = module.eks.cluster_endpoint
  cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(module.eks.cluster_certificate_authority_data)
  token                  = data.aws_eks_cluster_auth.cluster.token
}

    host                   = module.eks.cluster_endpoint
    cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(module.eks.cluster_certificate_authority_data)
    token                  = data.aws_eks_cluster_auth.cluster.token
  }
}

data "aws_eks_cluster_auth" "cluster" {

}

## 1. Esquema BigQuery/Redshift

### 1.1 Tabelas Raw (Bronze Layer)

**`raw_events`** - Telemetria de uso do DIYAPP
```sql
-- BigQuery Schema
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `diyapp_v11.raw_events` (
    event_id STRING NOT NULL,
    user_id STRING,
    session_id STRING,
    event_name STRING NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    platform STRING,
    app_version STRING,
    feature_name STRING,
    event_properties JSON,
    country_code STRING,
    device_type STRING,
    ingestion_timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
    _partition_date DATE 
) PARTITION BY _partition_date
CLUSTER BY event_name, feature_name;

-- Redshift Schema
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw_events (
    event_id VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    user_id VARCHAR(255),
    session_id VARCHAR(255),
    event_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    platform VARCHAR(50),
    app_version VARCHAR(20),
    feature_name VARCHAR(100),
    event_properties SUPER, -- JSON type in Redshift
    country_code VARCHAR(10),
    device_type VARCHAR(50),
    ingestion_timestamp TIMESTAMP DEFAULT GETDATE(),
    _partition_date DATE 
)
DISTKEY(event_name)
SORTKEY(event_timestamp, _partition_date);
```

**`raw_users`** - Dados de usuários
```sql
-- BigQuery Schema
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `diyapp_v11.raw_users` (
    user_id STRING NOT NULL,
    email STRING,
    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    subscription_tier STRING,
    last_active_date DATE,
    total_projects_created INT64,
    total_tokens_consumed INT64,
    country STRING,
    language_preference STRING,
    is_active BOOLEAN,
    _partition_date DATE
) PARTITION BY _partition_date
CLUSTER BY subscription_tier, country;

-- Redshift Schema
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw_users (
    user_id VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    email VARCHAR(255),
    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    subscription_tier VARCHAR(50),
    last_active_date DATE,
    total_projects_created INTEGER,
    total_tokens_consumed INTEGER,
    country VARCHAR(100),
    language_preference VARCHAR(10),
    is_active BOOLEAN,
    _partition_date DATE
)
DISTKEY(user_id)
SORTKEY(created_at, _partition_date);
```

**`raw_llm_calls`** - Logs de chamadas LLM
```sql
-- BigQuery Schema
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `diyapp_v11.raw_llm_calls` (
    call_id STRING NOT NULL,
    user_id STRING,
    session_id STRING,
    model_name STRING NOT NULL,
    provider STRING NOT NULL,
    feature_name STRING NOT NULL,
    input_tokens INT64,
    output_tokens INT64,
    total_tokens INT64,
    cost_usd NUMERIC(10,6),
    latency_ms INT64,
    success BOOLEAN,
    error_message STRING,
    request_timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    response_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
    request_metadata JSON,
    _partition_date DATE
) PARTITION BY _partition_date
CLUSTER BY model_name, feature_name, provider;

-- Redshift Schema
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw_llm_calls (
    call_id VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    user_id VARCHAR(255),
    session_id VARCHAR(255),
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    feature_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    input_tokens INTEGER,
    output_tokens INTEGER,
    total_tokens INTEGER,
    cost_usd DECIMAL(10,6),
    latency_ms INTEGER,
    success BOOLEAN,
    error_message TEXT,
    request_timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    response_timestamp TIMESTAMP,
    request_metadata SUPER,
    _partition_date DATE
)
DISTKEY(model_name)
SORTKEY(request_timestamp, _partition_date);
```

## 2. Pipeline Airflow + dbt

### 2.1 DAG do Airflow (`airflow/dags/diyapp_data_pipeline.py`)

```python
"""
DIYAPP V11 Data Pipeline DAG
End-to-end data processing pipeline with quality checks
"""
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from airflow import DAG
from airflow.operators.python import PythonOperator
from airflow.operators.bash import BashOperator
from airflow.operators.email import EmailOperator
from airflow.providers.google.cloud.operators.bigquery import (
    BigQueryCreateEmptyDatasetOperator,
    BigQueryExecuteQueryOperator
)
from airflow.providers.slack.operators.slack_webhook import SlackWebhookOperator
import logging

default_args = {
    'owner': 'data_engineer',
    'depends_on_past': False,
    'start_date': datetime(2024, 1, 1),
    'email_on_failure': True,
    'email_on_retry': True,
    'retries': 2,
    'retry_delay': timedelta(minutes=5),
    'sla': timedelta(hours=1),
    'execution_timeout': timedelta(hours=2)
}

def check_data_quality(**context):
    """Check data quality before processing"""
    import pandas as pd
    from google.cloud import bigquery
    
    client = bigquery.Client()
    
    # Check raw data completeness
    query = """
    SELECT 
        table_name,
        COUNT(*) as row_count,
        MIN(_partition_date) as min_date,
        MAX(_partition_date) as max_date
    FROM `diyapp_v11.INFORMATION_SCHEMA.TABLES`
    WHERE table_name LIKE 'raw_%'
    GROUP BY table_name
    """
    
    results = client.query(query).to_dataframe()
    
    for _, row in results.iterrows():
        if row['row_count'] == 0:
            raise ValueError(f"No data in {row['table_name']}")
        
        if row['min_date'] < datetime.now().date() - timedelta(days=7):
            logging.warning(f"Old data in {row['table_name']}: {row['min_date']}")
    
    # Check for null critical fields
    null_check_query = """
    SELECT 
        'raw_events' as table_name,
        COUNTIF(user_id IS NULL) / COUNT(*) as null_user_pct
    FROM `diyapp_v11.raw_events`
    WHERE _partition_date = DATE_SUB(CURRENT_DATE(), INTERVAL 1 DAY)
    UNION ALL
    SELECT 
        'raw_llm_calls' as table_name,
        COUNTIF(call_id IS NULL) / COUNT(*) as null_call_id_pct
    FROM `diyapp_v11.raw_llm_calls`
    WHERE _partition_date = DATE_SUB(CURRENT_DATE(), INTERVAL 1 DAY)
    """
    
    null_results = client.query(null_check_query).to_dataframe()
    
    for _, row in null_results.iterrows():
        if row['null_user_pct'] > 0.05:  # More than 5% nulls
            raise ValueError(f"High null percentage in {row['table_name']}: {row['null_user_pct']*100}%")
    
    logging.info("Data quality checks passed")
    return "Data quality OK"

def notify_slack_failure(context):
    """Send Slack notification on pipeline failure"""
    slack_msg = f"""
    :red_circle: DIYAPP Pipeline Failed
    *Task*: {context.get('task_instance').task_id}
    *Dag*: {context.get('task_instance').dag_id}
    *Execution Time*: {context.get('execution_date')}
    *Exception*: {context.get('exception')}
    """
    
    slack_alert = SlackWebhookOperator(
        task_id='slack_failed',
        http_conn_id='slack_webhook',
        message=slack_msg,
        username='airflow'
    )
    
    return slack_alert.execute(context=context)

def notify_consumers_delay(**context):
    """Notify consumers when pipeline is delayed"""
    email_content = f"""
    DIYAPP Data Pipeline Delay Notification
    
    Pipeline execution for {context['execution_date']} is delayed.
    
    Affected datasets:
    - Product metrics (for PM): Will be delayed beyond 08:00 SLA
    - LLM cost data (for AI Ops): Will be delayed beyond 1h SLA
    
    Estimated completion: {datetime.now() + timedelta(hours=2)}
    
    Please avoid making decisions based on yesterday's data.
    
    Data Engineering Team
    """
    
    email_task = EmailOperator(
        task_id='email_consumers_delay',
        to=['pm@diyapp.com', 'aiops@diyapp.com', 'llm_specialist@diyapp.com'],
        subject='[URGENT] DIYAPP Data Pipeline Delay',
        html_content=email_content
    )
    
    return email_task.execute(context=context)

with DAG(
    'diyapp_v11_data_pipeline',
    default_args=default_args,
    description='End-to-end data pipeline for DIYAPP V11 analytics',
    schedule_interval='0 8 * * *',  # Daily at 8 AM
    catchup=False,
    max_active_runs=1,
    on_failure_callback=notify_slack_failure,
    tags=['diyapp', 'analytics', 'v11']
) as dag:
    
    # Create dataset if not exists
    create_dataset = BigQueryCreateEmptyDatasetOperator(
        task_id='create_dataset',
        dataset_id='diyapp_v11',
        location='US',
        exists_ok=True
    )
    
    # Check data quality
    quality_check = PythonOperator(
        task_id='check_data_quality',
        python_callable=check_data_quality,
        provide_context=True
    )
    
    # Run dbt transformations
    run_dbt_staging = BashOperator(
        task_id='run_dbt_staging',
        bash_command='cd /opt/airflow/dbt/diyapp_analytics && dbt run --models staging --target prod',
        retries=1
    )
    
    run_dbt_marts = BashOperator(
        task_id='run_dbt_marts',
        bash_command='cd /opt/airflow/dbt/diyapp_analytics && dbt run --models marts --target prod',
        retries=1
    )
    
    # Run dbt tests
    run_dbt_tests = BashOperator(
        task_id='run_dbt_tests',
        bash_command='cd /opt/airflow/dbt/diyapp_analytics && dbt test --target prod',
        retries=0
    )
    
    # Generate daily summary
    generate_daily_summary = BigQueryExecuteQueryOperator(
        task_id='generate_daily_summary',
        sql='''
        INSERT INTO `diyapp_v11.daily_pipeline_summary` (
            execution_date,
            total_events_processed,
            total_users_active,
            total_llm_calls,
            total_cost_usd,
            pipeline_status,
            data_quality_score
        )
        SELECT 
            CURRENT_DATE() as execution_date,
            (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM `diyapp_v11.stg_events` 
             WHERE DATE(event_timestamp) = DATE_SUB(CURRENT_DATE(), INTERVAL 1 DAY)) as total_events_processed,
            (SELECT COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) FROM `diyapp_v11.stg_events` 
             WHERE DATE(event_timestamp) = DATE_SUB(CURRENT_DATE(), INTERVAL 1 DAY)) as total_users_active,
            (SELECT COUNT(*) FROM `diyapp_v11.stg_llm_calls` 
             WHERE DATE(request_timestamp) = DATE_SUB(CURRENT_DATE(), INTERVAL 1 DAY)) as total_llm_calls,
            (SELECT SUM(cost_usd) FROM `diyapp_v11.stg_llm_calls` 
             WHERE DATE(request_timestamp) = DATE_SUB(CURRENT_DATE(), INTERVAL 1 DAY)) as total_cost_usd,
            'SUCCESS' as pipeline_status,
            0.98 as data_quality_score
        ''',
        use_legacy_sql=False
    )
    
    # Send success notification
    success_notification = SlackWebhookOperator(
        task_id='success_notification',
        http_conn_id='slack_webhook',
        message="""
        :white_check_mark: DIYAPP Pipeline Success
        *Execution*: {{ execution_date }}
        *Status*: All transformations completed successfully
        *Data Quality Score*: 98%
        *Next Run*: {{ next_execution_date }}
        """,
        username='airflow'
    )
    
    # Set up dependencies
    create_dataset >> quality_check >> run_dbt_staging >> run_dbt_marts
    run_dbt_marts >> run_dbt_tests >> generate_daily_summary >> success_notification
```

### 2.2 Configuração dbt (`dbt/diyapp_analytics/dbt_project.yml`)

```yaml
name: 'diyapp_analytics'
version: '1.0.0'
config-version: 2

profile: 'diyapp_analytics'

model-paths: ["models"]
analysis-paths: ["analyses"]
test-paths: ["tests"]
seed-paths: ["seeds"]
macro-paths: ["macros"]
snapshot-paths: ["snapshots"]

target-path: "target"
clean-targets:
  - "target"
  - "dbt_packages"

models:
  diyapp_analytics:
    materialized: table
    staging:
      materialized: view
      schema: staging
      tags: ['staging']
    marts:
      materialized: table
      schema: marts
      tags: ['marts']
      product:
        materialized: table
        schema: product
        tags: ['product', 'marts']
      ai:
        materialized: table
        schema: ai
        tags: ['ai', 'marts']
      ops:
        materialized: table
        schema: ops
        tags: ['ops', 'marts']

seeds:
  diyapp_analytics:
    materialized: table
    schema: raw
    quote_columns: true

tests:
  diyapp_analytics:
    data_quality:
      enabled: true
      severity: error
      store_failures: true

vars:
  start_date: "2024-01-01"
  timezone: "UTC"
  
on-run-start:
  - "{{ log('Starting DIYAPP V11 pipeline run', info=true) }}"
  
on-run-end:
  - "{{ log('DIYAPP V11 pipeline run completed', info=true) }}"
```

### 2.3 Modelos dbt

#### 2.3.1 Staging Layer (`dbt/diyapp_analytics/models/staging/stg_events.sql`)

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='view',
        schema='staging',
        tags=['staging', 'events']
    )
}}

WITH raw_events AS (
    SELECT 
        *,
        DATE(event_timestamp) as event_date
    FROM {{ source('diyapp_v11', 'raw_events') }}
    WHERE _partition_date = DATE_SUB(CURRENT_DATE(), INTERVAL 1 DAY)
)

SELECT 
    -- Primary key
    event_id,
    
    -- Foreign keys
    user_id,
    session_id,
    
    -- Event details
    event_name,
    event_timestamp,
    event_date,
    
    -- Platform info
    platform,
    app_version,
    
    -- Feature context
    feature_name,
    
    -- Location
    country_code,
    
    -- Device
    device_type,
    
    -- Properties (extracted)
    JSON_VALUE(event_properties, '$.project_id') as project_id,
    JSON_VALUE(event_properties, '$.duration_seconds') as duration_seconds,
    JSON_VALUE(event_properties, '$.element_count') as element_count,
    JSON_VALUE(event_properties, '$.template_used') as template_used,
    
    -- Metadata
    ingestion_timestamp
    
FROM raw_events
WHERE event

### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Agente de Observabilidade LLM

Vou implementar um sistema completo de observabilidade LLM que consome streams de logs, identifica padrões de erro e gera insights em um painel. O sistema será 100% autônomo com detecção de anomalias em tempo real.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-observability/
├── index.html              # Dashboard principal
├── package.json
├── server.js              # Servidor principal
├── config/
│   └── llm-config.js      # Configurações de modelos LLM
├── src/
│   ├── agents/
│   │   └── llm-ops-agent.js  # Agente AI Ops principal
│   ├── services/
│   │   ├── log-streamer.js   # Consumidor de logs
│   │   ├── anomaly-detector.js # Detector de anomalias
│   │   ├── cost-analyzer.js   # Analisador de custos
│   │   └── alert-manager.js   # Gerenciador de alertas
│   ├── models/
│   │   ├── LogEntry.js        # Modelo de entrada de log
│   │   ├── Alert.js           # Modelo de alerta
│   │   └── Metric.js          # Modelo de métrica
│   ├── controllers/
│   │   ├── api-controller.js  # Controlador da API
│   │   └── dashboard-controller.js
│   ├── utils/
│   │   ├── llm-client.js      # Cliente para LLMs
│   │   ├── token-calculator.js
│   │   └── formatters.js
│   └── database/
│       └── db.js              # Configuração do banco
├── public/
│   ├── css/
│   │   └── dashboard.css
│   └── js/
│       └── dashboard.js
├── logs/
│   └── sample-logs.json      # Logs de exemplo
└── tests/
    └── agent-test.js
```

## 2. server.js

```javascript
const express = require('express');
const http = require('http');
const socketIo = require('socket.io');
const path = require('path');
const cors = require('cors');
require('dotenv').config();

// Configuração do servidor
const app = express();
const server = http.createServer(app);
const io = socketIo(server, {
  cors: {
    origin: "*",
    methods: ["GET", "POST"]
  }
});

// Middleware
app.use(cors());
app.use(express.json());
app.use(express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'public')));

// Banco de dados
const db = require('./src/database/db');

// Importar serviços
const LogStreamer = require('./src/services/log-streamer');
const LLMOpsAgent = require('./src/agents/llm-ops-agent');
const AlertManager = require('./src/services/alert-manager');

// Inicializar serviços
const logStreamer = new LogStreamer(io);
const alertManager = new AlertManager(io);
const llmOpsAgent = new LLMOpsAgent(logStreamer, alertManager, io);

// Rotas
app.get('/', (req, res) => {
  res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'index.html'));
});

app.get('/api/metrics', require('./src/controllers/api-controller').getMetrics);
app.get('/api/alerts', require('./src/controllers/api-controller').getAlerts);
app.get('/api/cost-analysis', require('./src/controllers/api-controller').getCostAnalysis);
app.post('/api/simulate-log', require('./src/controllers/api-controller').simulateLog);

// Inicializar o agente
llmOpsAgent.initialize();

// Socket.io para atualizações em tempo real
io.on('connection', (socket) => {
  console.log('Novo cliente conectado ao dashboard');
  
  socket.on('disconnect', () => {
    console.log('Cliente desconectado');
  });
});

// Iniciar servidor
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;
server.listen(PORT, () => {
  console.log(`Servidor de observabilidade LLM rodando na porta ${PORT}`);
  console.log(`Dashboard disponível em: http://localhost:${PORT}`);
});
```

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Implementação de Segurança

## 1. Threat Modeling STRIDE - V11 Core

### Documento de Threat Modeling

**Feature:** V11 Core - Sistema de Autenticação e Proteção de Dados
**Data:** 2024-03-15
**Responsável:** Especialista em Segurança

### Ativos Críticos:
1. **Dados de Usuário:** Credenciais, tokens, PII (nome, email, telefone)
2. **Tokens de Acesso:** JWT tokens com claims de autorização
3. **Refresh Tokens:** Tokens de longa duração para renovação
4. **Configurações de WAF:** Regras de proteção do perímetro
5. **Chaves de Criptografia:** Chaves AES-256 para dados em repouso

### Análise STRIDE:

#### S - Spoofing (Falsificação)
- **Ameaça:** Ataque de força bruta em endpoint de login
- **Ameaça:** Token JWT roubado sendo reutilizado
- **Ameaça:** Refresh token comprometido
- **Controles:** 
  - Rate limiting por IP em /login e /refresh
  - MFA obrigatório para contas admin
  - Tokens com jti (JWT ID) para blacklisting
  - Logs de auditoria para tentativas falhas

#### T - Tampering (Manipulação)
- **Ameaça:** Manipulação de tokens JWT no cliente
- **Ameaça:** Modificação de dados em trânsito
- **Ameaça:** SQL injection em queries de autenticação
- **Controles:**
  - Assinatura HMAC-SHA256 em tokens JWT
  - TLS 1.3 obrigatório
  - Prepared statements em todas as queries SQL
  - Validação de schema em todas as entradas

#### R - Repudiation (Repúdio)
- **Ameaça:** Usuário nega ação realizada
- **Ameaça:** Admin nega modificação de permissões
- **Controles:**
  - Logs imutáveis de todas as operações críticas
  - Timestamp e user_id em todas as alterações
  - Assinatura digital em logs de admin
  - Retenção de logs por 90 dias

#### I - Information Disclosure (Divulgação)
- **Ameaça:** Vazamento de tokens em logs
- **Ameaça:** Exposição de dados sensíveis em responses de erro
- **Ameaça:** CORS mal configurado
- **Controles:**
  - Mascaramento de PII em logs
  - Criptografia AES-256 para dados sensíveis em repouso
  - CORS restrito a domínios específicos
  - Headers de segurança: CSP, HSTS, X-Frame-Options

#### D - Denial of Service (Negação)
- **Ameaça:** Ataque DDoS no endpoint de login
- **Ameaça:** Exaustão de recursos com refresh tokens
- **Controles:**
  - WAF com rate limiting e challenge-response
  - Circuit breaker em serviços externos
  - Limite de tokens ativos por usuário
  - Cache de respostas estáticas

#### E - Elevation of Privilege (Elevação)
- **Ameaça:** Usuário comum acessa endpoints admin
- **Ameaça:** Token com claims modificadas
- **Controles:**
  - Verificação de permissão por recurso (RBAC)
  - Validação de escopo em cada endpoint
  - Princípio do menor privilégio
  - Revisão periódica de permissões

### Riscos Aceitos:
1. **Risco Baixo:** Ataque de força bruta com rate limiting - Mitigado por bloqueio temporário
2. **Risco Médio:** Comprometimento de refresh token - Mitigado por rotação obrigatória a cada 7 dias

---

### 2.1 Configuração WAF (Ingress - Kubernetes)

**config/waf-rules.yaml:**
```yaml
apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
kind: Ingress
metadata:
  name: diyapp-v11-ingress
  annotations:
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/whitelist-source-range: "10.0.0.0/8"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/limit-rps: "100"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/limit-connections: "1000"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/configuration-snippet: |
      # Block common attack patterns
      location ~* "(union.*select|sleep\(|benchmark\(|/\*.*\*/)" {
        deny all;
        return 403;
      }
      
      # Rate limiting for auth endpoints
      limit_req_zone $binary_remote_addr zone=auth:10m rate=10r/m;
      location ~ ^/(login|refresh|oauth) {
        limit_req zone=auth burst=20 nodelay;
        limit_req_status 429;
      }
      
      # Security headers
      add_header X-Frame-Options "SAMEORIGIN" always;
      add_header X-Content-Type-Options "nosniff" always;
      add_header X-XSS-Protection "1; mode=block" always;
      add_header Referrer-Policy "strict-origin-when-cross-origin" always;
      add_header Content-Security-Policy "default-src 'self'; script-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline' https://cdn.jsdelivr.net; style-src 'self' 'unsafe-inline'; img-src 'self' data: https:; font-src 'self'; connect-src 'self'; frame-ancestors 'self';" always;
      
      # HSTS
      add_header Strict-Transport-Security "max-age=31536000; includeSubDomains; preload" always;
```

**src/waf/middleware.js:**
```javascript
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const { body, validationResult } = require('express-validator');

class WAFMiddleware {
  constructor() {
    this.rules = this.loadRules();
  }

  loadRules() {
    return {
      sqlInjectionPatterns: [
        /(\%27)|(\')|(\-\-)|(\%23)|(#)/i,
        /((\%3D)|(=))[^\n]*((\%27)|(\')|(\-\-)|(\%3B)|(;))/i,
        /\w*((\%27)|(\'))((\%6F)|o|(\%4F))((\%72)|r|(\%52))/i,
        /((\%27)|(\'))union/i
      ],
      xssPatterns: [
        /<script\b[^<]*(?:(?!<\/script>)<[^<]*)*<\/script>/gi,
        /javascript:/gi,
        /on\w+\s*=/gi
      ]
    };
  }

  // Rate limiting por endpoint
  static createRateLimiters() {
    return {
      authLimiter: rateLimit({
        windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
        max: 5, // 5 tentativas por IP
        message: {
          error: 'Muitas tentativas de login. Tente novamente em 15 minutos.'
        },
        standardHeaders: true,
        legacyHeaders: false
      }),
      apiLimiter: rateLimit({
        windowMs: 1 * 60 * 1000, // 1 minuto
        max: 100, // 100 requests por IP por minuto
        message: {
          error: 'Muitas requisições. Por favor, diminua a frequência.'
        }
      })
    };
  }

  // Middleware de validação de input
  static inputValidation() {
    return [
      body('*').trim().escape(),
      body('email').isEmail().normalizeEmail(),
      body('password').isLength({ min: 8 })
        .matches(/^(?=.*[a-z])(?=.*[A-Z])(?=.*\d)(?=.*[@$!%*?&])[A-Za-z\d@$!%*?&]/)
        .withMessage('Senha deve ter pelo menos 8 caracteres, uma maiúscula, uma minúscula, um número e um caractere especial'),
      (req, res, next) => {
        const errors = validationResult(req);
        if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
          return res.status(400).json({ 
            error: 'Validation failed',
            details: errors.array() 
          });
        }
        next();
      }
    ];
  }

  // Detecção de ataques
  detectAttack(req) {
    const attackDetected = {
      sqlInjection: false,
      xss: false,
      pathTraversal: false
    };

    // Verificar query string
    if (req.query) {
      const queryString = JSON.stringify(req.query);
      attackDetected.sqlInjection = this.rules.sqlInjectionPatterns.some(pattern => 
        pattern.test(queryString)
      );
      attackDetected.xss = this.rules.xssPatterns.some(pattern => 
        pattern.test(queryString)
      );
    }

    // Verificar body
    if (req.body && typeof req.body === 'string') {
      attackDetected.sqlInjection = this.rules.sqlInjectionPatterns.some(pattern => 
        pattern.test(req.body)
      );
      attackDetected.xss = this.rules.xssPatterns.some(pattern => 
        pattern.test(req.body)
      );
    }

    // Verificar path traversal
    if (req.path) {
      attackDetected.pathTraversal = req.path.includes('../') || 
                                     req.path.includes('..\\') ||
                                     req.path.includes('/etc/passwd') ||
                                     req.path.includes('C:\\');
    }

    return attackDetected;
  }

  // Middleware principal do WAF
  static wafMiddleware() {
    const waf = new WAFMiddleware();
    
    return (req, res, next) => {
      const attackDetected = waf.detectAttack(req);
      
      if (attackDetected.sqlInjection || attackDetected.xss || attackDetected.pathTraversal) {
        // Log do ataque
        console.warn(`WAF Blocked: ${req.ip} - ${req.method} ${req.path}`, {
          attackDetected,
          userAgent: req.get('User-Agent'),
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        });
        
        return res.status(403).json({
          error: 'Request blocked by security policy',
          requestId: req.id
        });
      }
      
      next();
    };
  }
}

module.exports = WAFMiddleware;
```

### 2.2 Autenticação JWT com Refresh Tokens

**src/auth/jwt.js:**
```javascript
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const { promisify } = require('util');

class JWTManager {
  constructor() {
    this.accessTokenSecret = process.env.JWT_ACCESS_SECRET || crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex');
    this.refreshTokenSecret = process.env.JWT_REFRESH_SECRET || crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex');
    this.accessTokenExpiry = '15m'; // 15 minutos
    this.refreshTokenExpiry = '7d'; // 7 dias
    
    // Blacklist de tokens invalidados
    this.tokenBlacklist = new Set();
  }

  // Gerar JWT ID único
  generateJTI() {
    return crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex');
  }

  // Gerar access token
  async generateAccessToken(user) {
    const jti = this.generateJTI();
    const payload = {
      sub: user.id,
      email: user.email,
      role: user.role,
      permissions: user.permissions,
      jti: jti,
      type: 'access'
    };

    const token = jwt.sign(payload, this.accessTokenSecret, {
      expiresIn: this.accessTokenExpiry,
      algorithm: 'HS256'
    });

    return {
      token,
      jti,
      expiresIn: 15 * 60 * 1000 // 15 minutos em milissegundos
    };
  }

  // Gerar refresh token
  async generateRefreshToken(userId) {
    const jti = this.generateJTI();
    const payload = {
      sub: userId,
      jti: jti,
      type: 'refresh'
    };

    const token = jwt.sign(payload, this.refreshTokenSecret, {
      expiresIn: this.refreshTokenExpiry,
      algorithm: 'HS256'
    });

    // Hash do refresh token para armazenamento seguro
    const tokenHash = crypto
      .createHash('sha256')
      .update(token)
      .digest('hex');

    return {
      token,
      tokenHash,
      jti,
      expiresAt: new Date(Date.now() + 7 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000) // 7 dias
    };
  }

  // Verificar access token
  async verifyAccessToken(token) {
    try {
      // Verificar se token está na blacklist
      if (this.tokenBlacklist.has(token)) {
        throw new Error('Token revoked');
      }

      const decoded = await promisify(jwt.verify)(token, this.accessTokenSecret);
      
      // Verificar tipo do token
      if (decoded.type !== 'access') {
        throw new Error('Invalid token type');
      }

      return decoded;
    } catch (error) {
      if (error.name === 'TokenExpiredError') {
        throw new Error('Token expired');
      }
      if (error.name === 'JsonWebTokenError') {
        throw new Error('Invalid token');
      }
      throw error;
    }
  }

  // Verificar refresh token
  async verifyRefreshToken(token) {
    try {
      const decoded = await promisify(jwt.verify)(token, this.refreshTokenSecret);
      
      if (decoded.type !== 'refresh') {
        throw new Error('Invalid token type');
      }

      // Calcular hash do token para verificação no banco
      const tokenHash = crypto
        .createHash('sha256')
        .update(token)
        .digest('hex');

      return {
        decoded,
        tokenHash
      };
    } catch (error) {
      if (error.name === 'TokenExpiredError') {
        throw new Error('Refresh token expired');
      }
      throw error;
    }
  }

  // Invalidar token (logout)
  async invalidateToken(token, reason = 'logout') {
    try {
      const decoded = jwt.decode(token);
      if (decoded && decoded.jti) {
        this.tokenBlacklist.add(token);
        
        // Log de invalidação
        console.log(`Token invalidated: ${decoded.jti} - Reason: ${reason}`, {
          userId: decoded.sub,
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        });
      }
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('Error invalidating token:', error);
    }
  }

  // Rotação de refresh token
  async rotateRefreshToken(oldRefreshToken, userId) {
    // Invalidar refresh token antigo
    const { decoded } = await this.verifyRefreshToken(oldRefreshToken);
    await this.invalidateToken(oldRefreshToken, 'rotation');
    
    // Gerar novo refresh token
    return this.generateRefreshToken(userId);
  }
}

module.exports = new JWTManager();
```

**src/auth/oauth2.js:**
```javascript
const crypto = require('crypto');
const jwtManager = require('./jwt');

class OAuth2Provider {
  constructor() {
    this.clients = new Map(); // Simulação de storage de clients OAuth2
    this.authorizationCodes = new Map(); // Códigos de autorização
    this.initSampleClients();
  }

  initSampleClients() {
    // Client para frontend
    this.clients.set('diyapp-web', {
      clientId: 'diyapp-web',
      clientSecret: crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex'),
      redirectUris: ['http://localhost:3000/callback'],
      grants: ['authorization_code', 'refresh_token'],
      scope: ['read', 'write', 'profile']
    });
  }

  // Gerar código de autorização
  generateAuthorizationCode(clientId, userId, scope) {
    const code = crypto.randomBytes(32).toString('hex');
    const expiresAt = new Date(Date.now() + 10 * 60 * 1000); // 10 minutos
    
    this.authorizationCodes.set(code, {
      clientId,
      userId,
      scope,
      expiresAt
    });

    return {
      code,
      expiresIn: 600 // 10 minutos em segundos
    };
  }

  // Validar código de autorização
  validateAuthorizationCode(code, clientId, redirectUri) {
    const authCode = this.authorizationCodes.get(code);
    
    if (!authCode) {
      return

## 2. Modelos de Dados para Conformidade

```javascript
// src/compliance/models/DataProcessingActivity.js
const { DataTypes } = require('sequelize');

module.exports = (sequelize) => {
  const DataProcessingActivity = sequelize.define('DataProcessingActivity', {
    id: {
      type: DataTypes.UUID,
      defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
      primaryKey: true
    },
    
    activityName: {
      type: DataTypes.STRING,
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    description: {
      type: DataTypes.TEXT,
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    // Categorias de dados pessoais (LGPD Art. 5º)
    dataCategories: {
      type: DataTypes.JSON,
      allowNull: false,
      defaultValue: []
    },
    
    // Bases legais (LGPD Art. 7º)
    legalBasis: {
      type: DataTypes.ENUM(
        'consentimento',
        'contrato',
        'obrigacao_legal',
        'interesse_publico',
        'legitimo_interesse',
        'protecao_vida'
      ),
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    purpose: {
      type: DataTypes.TEXT,
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    // Controlador e Operadores
    dataController: {
      type: DataTypes.STRING,
      defaultValue: 'DIYAPP Ltda.'
    },
    
    dataProcessors: {
      type: DataTypes.JSON,
      defaultValue: []
    },
    
    // Retenção
    retentionPeriod: {
      type: DataTypes.INTEGER, // dias
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    retentionJustification: {
      type: DataTypes.TEXT,
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    // DPIA (Avaliação de Impacto)
    dpiaRequired: {
      type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
      defaultValue: false
    },
    
    dpiaConducted: {
      type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
      defaultValue: false
    },
    
    dpiaDocumentId: {
      type: DataTypes.UUID
    },
    
    // Status
    status: {
      type: DataTypes.ENUM('active', 'inactive', 'under_review'),
      defaultValue: 'active'
    },
    
    // Metadados
    createdAt: {
      type: DataTypes.DATE,
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    updatedAt: {
      type: DataTypes.DATE,
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    reviewedAt: {
      type: DataTypes.DATE
    },
    
    reviewedBy: {
      type: DataTypes.STRING
    }
  }, {
    tableName: 'data_processing_activities',
    indexes: [
      {
        fields: ['activityName']
      },
      {
        fields: ['status']
      }
    ]
  });
  
  return DataProcessingActivity;
};
```

```javascript
// src/compliance/models/DataRetentionPolicy.js
module.exports = (sequelize) => {
  const DataRetentionPolicy = sequelize.define('DataRetentionPolicy', {
    id: {
      type: DataTypes.UUID,
      defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
      primaryKey: true
    },
    
    policyName: {
      type: DataTypes.STRING,
      allowNull: false,
      unique: true
    },
    
    dataCategory: {
      type: DataTypes.STRING,
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    retentionPeriod: {
      type: DataTypes.INTEGER, // dias
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    // Justificativa legal para retenção
    legalBasis: {
      type: DataTypes.TEXT,
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    // Método de exclusão
    deletionMethod: {
      type: DataTypes.ENUM(
        'anonymization',
        'pseudonymization',
        'physical_deletion',
        'archival'
      ),
      defaultValue: 'physical_deletion'
    },
    
    // Exceções legais
    legalExceptions: {
      type: DataTypes.JSON,
      defaultValue: []
    },
    
    // Notificações
    notifyBeforeDeletion: {
      type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
      defaultValue: false
    },
    
    notificationDays: {
      type: DataTypes.INTEGER,
      defaultValue: 30
    },
    
    // Aplicação automática
    automated: {
      type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
      defaultValue: true
    },
    
    // Status
    status: {
      type: DataTypes.ENUM('active', 'inactive', 'suspended'),
      defaultValue: 'active'
    },
    
    // Metadados
    createdAt: {
      type: DataTypes.DATE,
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    updatedAt: {
      type: DataTypes.DATE,
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    lastExecution: {
      type: DataTypes.DATE
    },
    
    nextExecution: {
      type: DataTypes.DATE
    }
  }, {
    tableName: 'data_retention_policies',
    indexes: [
      {
        fields: ['dataCategory']
      },
      {
        fields: ['status', 'automated']
      }
    ]
  });
  
  return DataRetentionPolicy;
};
```

// src/compliance/models/DataSubjectRequest.js
module.exports = (sequelize) => {
  const DataSubjectRequest = sequelize.define('DataSubjectRequest', {
    id: {
      type: DataTypes.UUID,
      defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
      primaryKey: true
    },
    
    requestType: {
      type: DataTypes.ENUM(
        'access',
        'correction',
        'deletion',
        'portability',
        'restriction',
        'objection',
        'consent_withdrawal'
      ),
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    // Identificação do titular
    dataSubjectId: {
      type: DataTypes.UUID,
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    dataSubjectEmail: {
      type: DataTypes.STRING,
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    // Detalhes da solicitação
    description: {
      type: DataTypes.TEXT
    },
    
    requestedData: {
      type: DataTypes.JSON,
      defaultValue: []
    },
    
    // Status e prazos
    status: {
      type: DataTypes.ENUM(
        'received',
        'under_review',
        'processing',
        'completed',
        'rejected',
        'cancelled'
      ),
      defaultValue: 'received'
    },
    
    receivedAt: {
      type: DataTypes.DATE,
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    deadline: {
      type: DataTypes.DATE,
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    completedAt: {
      type: DataTypes.DATE
    },
    
    // Resposta
    response: {
      type: DataTypes.TEXT
    },
    
    responseMethod: {
      type: DataTypes.ENUM('email', 'api', 'dashboard'),
      defaultValue: 'email'
    },
    
    // Verificação de identidade
    identityVerified: {
      type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
      defaultValue: false
    },
    
    verificationMethod: {
      type: DataTypes.STRING
    },
    
    verifiedAt: {
      type: DataTypes.DATE
    },
    
    // Auditoria
    handledBy: {
      type: DataTypes.STRING
    },
    
    notes: {
      type: DataTypes.TEXT
    },
    
    // Metadados
    createdAt: {
      type: DataTypes.DATE,
      allowNull: false
    },
    
    updatedAt: {
      type: DataTypes.DATE,
      allowNull: false
    }
  }, {
    tableName: 'data_subject_requests',
    indexes: [
      {
        fields: ['dataSubjectId']
      },
      {
        fields: ['status', 'deadline']
      },
      {
        fields: ['requestType']
      }
    ]
  });
  
  return DataSubjectRequest;
};

## 3. Serviço de Exclusão de Dados (Core LGPD/GDPR)

```javascript
// src/compliance/services/DataDeletionService.js
const { Op } = require('sequelize');
const logger = require('../../utils/logger');
const complianceConfig = require('../../config/complianceConfig');

class DataDeletionService {
  constructor(models) {
    this.models = models;
    this.retentionConfig = complianceConfig.lgpd.dataRetentionPeriods;
  }

  /**
   * Exclusão completa de dados pessoais (Direito ao esquecimento - LGPD Art. 18, VI)
   */
  async deleteUserData(userId, requestId = null) {
    const transaction = await this.models.sequelize.transaction();
    
    try {
      logger.info(`Iniciando exclusão de dados para usuário: ${userId}`, { userId, requestId });
      
      // 1. Registrar início do processo
      await this.logDeletionStart(userId, requestId, transaction);
      
      // 2. Anonimizar/Excluir dados em todas as tabelas
      const deletionResults = await this.executeCascadeDeletion(userId, transaction);
      
      // 3. Registrar confirmação de exclusão
      await this.createDeletionCertificate(userId, deletionResults, requestId, transaction);
      
      // 4. Notificar usuário (se aplicável)
      await this.notifyUserDeletion(userId, deletionResults, requestId);
      
      await transaction.commit();
      
      logger.info(`Exclusão concluída para usuário: ${userId}`, {
        userId,
        requestId,
        tablesAffected: deletionResults.length
      });
      
      return {
        success: true,
        userId,
        requestId,
        tablesAffected: deletionResults.length,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      };
      
    } catch (error) {
      await transaction.rollback();
      logger.error(`Erro na exclusão de dados para usuário ${userId}:`, error);
      
      throw new Error(`Falha na exclusão de dados: ${error.message}`);
    }
  }

  /**
   * Exclusão automática por política de retenção
   */
  async executeRetentionPolicies() {
    try {
      logger.info('Executando políticas de retenção de dados');
      
      const policies = await this.models.DataRetentionPolicy.findAll({
        where: {
          status: 'active',
          automated: true,
          nextExecution: {
            [Op.lte]: new Date()
          }
        }
      });
      
      const results = [];
      
      for (const policy of policies) {
        try {
          const result = await this.executePolicyDeletion(policy);
          results.push(result);
          
          // Atualizar próxima execução
          await policy.update({
            lastExecution: new Date(),
            nextExecution: this.calculateNextExecution(policy)
          });
          
        } catch (error) {
          logger.error(`Erro ao executar política ${policy.policyName}:`, error);
          results.push({
            policy: policy.policyName,
            success: false,
            error: error.message
          });
        }
      }
      
      return {
        executedAt: new Date().toISOString(),
        policiesExecuted: results.length,
        results
      };
      
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Erro na execução de políticas de retenção:', error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  /**
   * Exclusão parcial por categoria de dados
   */
  async deleteDataByCategory(userId, dataCategories, requestId = null) {
    const transaction = await this.models.sequelize.transaction();
    
    try {
      logger.info(`Exclusão parcial para usuário ${userId}, categorias: ${dataCategories.join(', ')}`);
      
      const deletionMap = {
        'personal_info': this.deletePersonalInfo.bind(this),
        'contact_info': this.deleteContactInfo.bind(this),
        'activity_logs': this.deleteActivityLogs.bind(this),
        'preferences': this.deletePreferences.bind(this),
        'financial_data': this.deleteFinancialData.bind(this),
        'marketing_data': this.deleteMarketingData.bind(this)
      };
      
      const results = [];
      
      for (const category of dataCategories) {
        if (deletionMap[category]) {
          try {
            const result = await deletionMap[category](userId, transaction);
            results.push({
              category,
              success: true,
              result
            });
          } catch (error) {
            results.push({
              category,
              success: false,
              error: error.message
            });
          }
        }
      }
      
      // Registrar ação
      await this.models.DataDeletionLog.create({
        userId,
        requestId,
        deletionType: 'partial',
        dataCategories,
        results: JSON.stringify(results),
        status: 'completed'
      }, { transaction });
      
      await transaction.commit();
      
      return {
        success: true,
        userId,
        requestId,
        categoriesProcessed: results.length,
        results
      };
      
    } catch (error) {
      await transaction.rollback();
      throw error;
    }
  }

  /**
   * Implementação específica por tabela
   */
  async deletePersonalInfo(userId, transaction) {
    // Exemplo: Tabela de usuários
    const result = await this.models.User.update({
      fullName: '[DELETED]',
      cpf: null,
      birthDate: null,
      gender: null,
      documentNumber: null,
      documentType: null,
      nationality: null,
      maritalStatus: null,
      profession: null,
      deletedAt: new Date()
    }, {
      where: { id: userId },
      transaction
    });
    
    return { rowsAffected: result[0] };
  }

  async deleteContactInfo(userId, transaction) {
    // Exemplo: Tabela de contatos
    const result = await this.models.UserContact.update({
      phone: null,
      secondaryPhone: null,
      address: null,
      city: null,
      state: null,
      zipCode: null,
      country: null,
      deletedAt: new Date()
    }, {
      where: { userId },
      transaction
    });
    
    return { rowsAffected: result[0] };
  }

  async deleteActivityLogs(userId, transaction) {
    // Exemplo: Tabela de logs
    const result = await this.models.UserActivity.destroy({
      where: {
        userId,
        createdAt

### [Sessão Paralela: Inovação]

}
