## 1. Configuração Cypress E2E

### `test/e2e/cypress/cypress.config.js`

```javascript
const { defineConfig } = require('cypress')
const fs = require('fs')
const path = require('path')

module.exports = defineConfig({
  projectId: 'diyapp-v11',
  viewportWidth: 1920,
  viewportHeight: 1080,
  defaultCommandTimeout: 10000,
  requestTimeout: 10000,
  responseTimeout: 10000,
  video: true,
  videoCompression: 32,
  screenshotOnRunFailure: true,
  trashAssetsBeforeRuns: true,
  
  env: {
    baseUrl: process.env.CYPRESS_BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:3000',
    apiUrl: process.env.CYPRESS_API_URL || 'http://localhost:3001',
    adminUser: process.env.CYPRESS_ADMIN_USER || 'admin@diyapp.com',
    adminPassword: process.env.CYPRESS_ADMIN_PASSWORD || 'Admin123!',
    testUser: process.env.CYPRESS_TEST_USER || 'test@diyapp.com',
    testPassword: process.env.CYPRESS_TEST_PASSWORD || 'Test123!',
  },
  
  e2e: {
    setupNodeEvents(on, config) {
      // Gerar relatórios de cobertura
      on('task', {
        generateCoverageReport({ coverage }) {
          const reportDir = path.join(__dirname, '../../../reports/coverage')
          if (!fs.existsSync(reportDir)) {
            fs.mkdirSync(reportDir, { recursive: true })
          }
          
          const timestamp = new Date().toISOString().replace(/[:.]/g, '-')
          const reportFile = path.join(reportDir, `e2e-coverage-${timestamp}.json`)
          
          fs.writeFileSync(reportFile, JSON.stringify(coverage, null, 2))
          console.log(`Relatório de cobertura salvo em: ${reportFile}`)
          return null
        },
        
        log(message) {
          console.log(message)
          return null
        }
      })
      
      return config
    },
    
    specPattern: 'test/e2e/cypress/integration/**/*.spec.js',
    supportFile: 'test/e2e/cypress/support/e2e.js',
    experimentalRunAllSpecs: true,
  },
  
  retries: {
    runMode: 1,
    openMode: 0
  }
})
```

### `test/e2e/cypress/support/e2e.js`

```javascript
import './commands'

// Hooks globais
beforeEach(() => {
  // Limpar cookies e localStorage
  cy.clearCookies()
  cy.clearLocalStorage()
  
  // Log do teste atual
  cy.task('log', `Iniciando teste: ${Cypress.currentTest.title}`)
})

afterEach(() => {
  // Capturar screenshot em caso de falha
  if (Cypress.currentTest.state === 'failed') {
    const screenshotName = `${Cypress.currentTest.titlePath.join(' - ')} (failed)`
    cy.screenshot(screenshotName, { overwrite: true })
  }
})

after(() => {
  // Gerar relatório de cobertura
  const coverage = {
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    totalTests: Cypress.env('totalTests') || 0,
    passedTests: Cypress.env('passedTests') || 0,
    failedTests: Cypress.env('failedTests') || 0,
    testSuites: Cypress.env('testSuites') || []
  }
  
  cy.task('generateCoverageReport', { coverage })
})
```

### `test/e2e/cypress/support/commands.js`

```javascript
// Comandos customizados para DIYAPP V11

Cypress.Commands.add('login', (email, password) => {
  cy.visit('/login')
  cy.get('[data-testid="email-input"]').type(email)
  cy.get('[data-testid="password-input"]').type(password)
  cy.get('[data-testid="login-button"]').click()
  cy.url().should('include', '/dashboard')
  cy.get('[data-testid="user-menu"]').should('be.visible')
})

Cypress.Commands.add('logout', () => {
  cy.get('[data-testid="user-menu"]').click()
  cy.get('[data-testid="logout-button"]').click()
  cy.url().should('include', '/login')
})

Cypress.Commands.add('createProject', (projectName, projectType = 'web') => {
  cy.get('[data-testid="new-project-button"]').click()
  cy.get('[data-testid="project-name-input"]').type(projectName)
  cy.get(`[data-testid="project-type-${projectType}"]`).click()
  cy.get('[data-testid="create-project-button"]').click()
  cy.contains(projectName).should('be.visible')
})

Cypress.Commands.add('apiRequest', (method, endpoint, body = null, headers = {}) => {
  const defaultHeaders = {
    'Content-Type': 'application/json',
    'Authorization': `Bearer ${Cypress.env('apiToken')}`
  }
  
  return cy.request({
    method,
    url: `${Cypress.env('apiUrl')}${endpoint}`,
    body,
    headers: { ...defaultHeaders, ...headers },
    failOnStatusCode: false
  })
})
```

## 2. Testes E2E para Funcionalidades Herdadas V10

### `test/e2e/cypress/integration/authentication.spec.js`

```javascript
describe('Autenticação - Funcionalidades V10', () => {
  beforeEach(() => {
    cy.visit('/')
  })

  it('CT-001: Login com credenciais válidas', () => {
    cy.login(Cypress.env('testUser'), Cypress.env('testPassword'))
    cy.get('[data-testid="welcome-message"]').should('contain', 'Bem-vindo')
  })

  it('CT-002: Login com credenciais inválidas', () => {
    cy.visit('/login')
    cy.get('[data-testid="email-input"]').type('invalid@email.com')
    cy.get('[data-testid="password-input"]').type('wrongpassword')
    cy.get('[data-testid="login-button"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="error-message"]').should('contain', 'Credenciais inválidas')
  })

  it('CT-003: Recuperação de senha', () => {
    cy.visit('/forgot-password')
    cy.get('[data-testid="email-input"]').type(Cypress.env('testUser'))
    cy.get('[data-testid="submit-button"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="success-message"]').should('contain', 'E-mail enviado')
  })

  it('CT-004: Logout do sistema', () => {
    cy.login(Cypress.env('testUser'), Cypress.env('testPassword'))
    cy.logout()
  })

  it('CT-005: Sessão expirada redireciona para login', () => {
    cy.login(Cypress.env('testUser'), Cypress.env('testPassword'))
    
    // Simular expiração de token
    cy.window().then((win) => {
      win.localStorage.removeItem('auth_token')
    })
    
    cy.reload()
    cy.url().should('include', '/login')
  })
})
```

### `test/e2e/cypress/integration/project-management.spec.js`

```javascript
describe('Gerenciamento de Projetos - Funcionalidades V10', () => {
  before(() => {
    cy.login(Cypress.env('testUser'), Cypress.env('testPassword'))
  })

  after(() => {
    cy.logout()
  })

  it('CT-101: Criar novo projeto', () => {
    const projectName = `Test Project ${Date.now()}`
    cy.createProject(projectName, 'web')
    cy.get('[data-testid="project-list"]').should('contain', projectName)
  })

  it('CT-102: Editar projeto existente', () => {
    const projectName = `Edit Project ${Date.now()}`
    cy.createProject(projectName, 'web')
    
    cy.contains(projectName).click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="edit-project-button"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="project-name-input"]').clear().type(`${projectName} Editado`)
    cy.get('[data-testid="save-project-button"]').click()
    
    cy.contains(`${projectName} Editado`).should('be.visible')
  })

  it('CT-103: Excluir projeto', () => {
    const projectName = `Delete Project ${Date.now()}`
    cy.createProject(projectName, 'web')
    
    cy.contains(projectName).click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="delete-project-button"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="confirm-delete-button"]').click()
    
    cy.get('[data-testid="project-list"]').should('not.contain', projectName)
  })

  it('CT-104: Duplicar projeto', () => {
    const projectName = `Duplicate Project ${Date.now()}`
    cy.createProject(projectName, 'web')
    
    cy.contains(projectName).click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="duplicate-project-button"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="confirm-duplicate-button"]').click()
    
    cy.get('[data-testid="project-list"]').should('contain', `${projectName} - Cópia`)
  })

  it('CT-105: Filtrar projetos por tipo', () => {
    // Criar projetos de diferentes tipos
    cy.createProject(`Web Project ${Date.now()}`, 'web')
    cy.createProject(`Mobile Project ${Date.now()}`, 'mobile')
    cy.createProject(`API Project ${Date.now()}`, 'api')
    
    // Filtrar por tipo web
    cy.get('[data-testid="filter-web"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="project-list"] [data-project-type="web"]').should('have.length.at.least', 1)
    cy.get('[data-testid="project-list"] [data-project-type="mobile"]').should('not.exist')
  })
})
```

### `test/e2e/cypress/integration/code-editor.spec.js`

```javascript
describe('Editor de Código - Funcionalidades V10', () => {
  let projectId

  before(() => {
    cy.login(Cypress.env('testUser'), Cypress.env('testPassword'))
    
    // Criar projeto para testes
    const projectName = `Code Editor Test ${Date.now()}`
    cy.createProject(projectName, 'web')
    cy.contains(projectName).click()
    
    // Obter ID do projeto
    cy.url().then((url) => {
      projectId = url.split('/').pop()
    })
  })

  after(() => {
    cy.logout()
  })

  it('CT-201: Adicionar novo arquivo ao projeto', () => {
    cy.get('[data-testid="add-file-button"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="file-name-input"]').type('index.html')
    cy.get('[data-testid="file-type-select"]').select('html')
    cy.get('[data-testid="create-file-button"]').click()
    
    cy.get('[data-testid="file-tree"]').should('contain', 'index.html')
  })

  it('CT-202: Editar conteúdo do arquivo', () => {
    cy.get('[data-testid="file-tree"]').contains('index.html').click()
    
    // Usar o editor Monaco (ou similar)
    cy.get('.monaco-editor').click().type('{selectall}{del}')
    cy.get('.monaco-editor').type('<h1>Hello DIYAPP</h1>', { force: true })
    
    cy.get('[data-testid="save-file-button"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="save-success"]').should('be.visible')
  })

  it('CT-203: Renomear arquivo', () => {
    cy.get('[data-testid="file-tree"]').contains('index.html').rightclick()
    cy.get('[data-testid="rename-file-option"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="rename-input"]').clear().type('main.html{enter}')
    
    cy.get('[data-testid="file-tree"]').should('contain', 'main.html')
    cy.get('[data-testid="file-tree"]').should('not.contain', 'index.html')
  })

  it('CT-204: Excluir arquivo', () => {
    cy.get('[data-testid="file-tree"]').contains('main.html').rightclick()
    cy.get('[data-testid="delete-file-option"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="confirm-delete-button"]').click()
    
    cy.get('[data-testid="file-tree"]').should('not.contain', 'main.html')
  })

  it('CT-205: Preview do código em tempo real', () => {
    // Adicionar arquivo HTML
    cy.get('[data-testid="add-file-button"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="file-name-input"]').type('test.html')
    cy.get('[data-testid="file-type-select"]').select('html')
    cy.get('[data-testid="create-file-button"]').click()
    
    // Editar conteúdo
    cy.get('[data-testid="file-tree"]').contains('test.html').click()
    cy.get('.monaco-editor').click().type('{selectall}{del}')
    cy.get('.monaco-editor').type('<h1>Test Preview</h1><p>Conteúdo dinâmico</p>', { force: true })
    cy.get('[data-testid="save-file-button"]').click()
    
    // Verificar preview
    cy.get('[data-testid="preview-tab"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="preview-frame"]').its('0.contentDocument.body').should('contain', 'Test Preview')
  })
})
```

```javascript
describe('Colaboração em Tempo Real - Funcionalidades V10', () => {
  let projectId
  let shareLink

  before(() => {
    cy.login(Cypress.env('testUser'), Cypress.env('testPassword'))
    
    // Criar projeto para colaboração
    const projectName = `Collaboration Test ${Date.now()}`
    cy.createProject(projectName, 'web')
    cy.contains(projectName).click()
    
    cy.url().then((url) => {
      projectId = url.split('/').pop()
    })
  })

  it('CT-301: Compartilhar projeto com link público', () => {
    cy.get('[data-testid="share-project-button"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="generate-share-link"]').click()
    
    cy.get('[data-testid="share-link-input"]').invoke('val').then((link) => {
      shareLink = link
      expect(link).to.include('/share/')
    })
    
    cy.get('[data-testid="copy-link-button"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="copy-success"]').should('be.visible')
  })

  it('CT-302: Acessar projeto compartilhado (modo leitura)', () => {
    // Usar outra sessão para simular colaborador
    cy.origin(Cypress.env('baseUrl'), { args: { shareLink } }, ({ shareLink }) => {
      cy.visit(shareLink)
      cy.get('[data-testid="shared-project-view"]').should('be.visible')
      cy.get('[data-testid="editor"]').should('be.disabled')
    })
  })

  })

  it('CT-304: Chat em tempo real no projeto', () => {
    cy.get('[data-testid="open-chat-button"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="chat-window"]').should('be.visible')
    
    const message = `Test message ${Date.now()}`
    cy.get('[data-testid="chat-input"]').type(message)
    cy.get('[data-testid="send-message-button"]').click()
    
    cy.get('[data-testid="chat-messages"]').should('contain', message)
  })

  it('CT-305: Ver histórico de alterações', () => {
    // Fazer uma alteração
    cy.get('[data-testid="add-file-button"]').click()
    cy.get('[data-testid="file-name-input"]').type('history-test.js')
    cy.get('[data-testid="create-file-button

# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Documentação Diátaxis

## 1. Configuração Principal (mkdocs.yml)

```yaml
# mkdocs.yml
site_name: DIYAPP Evolution V11
site_description: Documentação completa da API DIYAPP V11 Core
site_url: https://docs.diyapp.com
repo_url: https://github.com/diyapp/diyapp-docs
repo_name: diyapp/diyapp-docs

theme:
  name: material
  features:
    - navigation.tabs
    - navigation.sections
    - toc.integrate
    - search.suggest
    - search.highlight
    - content.tabs.link
    - content.code.annotation
    - content.code.copy
  palette:
    - scheme: default
      primary: indigo
      accent: indigo
      toggle:
        icon: material/brightness-7
        name: Switch to dark mode
    - scheme: slate
      primary: indigo
      accent: indigo
      toggle:
        icon: material/brightness-4
        name: Switch to light mode

plugins:
  - search
  - mkdocstrings:
      handlers:
        python:
          paths: [src]
  - git-committers:
      repository: diyapp/diyapp-docs
      branch: main

markdown_extensions:
  - admonition
  - codehilite
  - pymdownx.superfences
  - pymdownx.tabbed:
      alternate_style: true
  - pymdownx.details
  - toc:
      permalink: true

nav:
  - Home: index.md
  - Tutorials:
    - Getting Started: tutorials/getting-started.md
    - First Integration: tutorials/first-integration.md
    - Advanced Workflows: tutorials/advanced-workflows.md
  - How-To Guides:
    - Authentication: how-to-guides/authentication.md
    - Webhook Setup: how-to-guides/webhook-setup.md
    - Error Handling: how-to-guides/error-handling.md
    - Deployment: how-to-guides/deployment.md
  - Reference:
    - API Reference: reference/api-reference.md
    - Error Codes: reference/error-codes.md
    - SDK: reference/sdk.md
  - Explanation:
    - Architecture: explanation/architecture.md
    - Core Concepts: explanation/concepts.md
    - Security Model: explanation/security-model.md
  - Changelog: changelog.md
```
